OpenvSwitch (OVS) >

OVS Source Build Oracle Linux 7 UEK4 Kernel

Contents

  1. 1 Summary
  2. 2 Steps
    1. 2.1 Install rpm-build
    2. 2.2 Install wget
    3. 2.3 Install openssl-devel
    4. 2.4 Get OpenvSwitch Install Bundle
    5. 2.5 Expand OpenvSwitch Install Bundle
    6. 2.6 Build OpenvSwitch RPM
    7. 2.7 Install OpenvSwitch RPM
    8. 2.8 Check if OpenvSwitch DB present and create if needed
    9. 2.9 Reboot Server
    10. 2.10 Verify OpenvSwitch Operation

Summary

Build OpenvSwitch from source on Oracle Linux 7 UEK4 kernel.

Steps

The steps are as shown below.

Install rpm-build

[root@uekulele1 ~]# yum -y install rpm-build
Loaded plugins: ulninfo
Package rpm-build-4.11.3-17.el7.x86_64 already installed and latest version
Nothing to do

Install wget

[root@uekulele1 SOURCES]# yum install wget

--> Finished Dependency Resolution

mv -f $depbase.Tpo $depbase.Plo

/bin/sh ./libtool --tag=CC --mode=compile gcc -std=gnu99 -DHAVE_CONFIG_H -I. -I ./include -I ./include -I ./lib -I ./lib -Wstrict-prototypes -Wall -Wextra -Wno-sign-compare -Wpointer-arith -Wswitch-enum -Wunused-parameter -Wbad-function-cast -Wcast-align -Wmissing-prototypes -Wmissing-field-initializers -fno-strict-aliasing -g -O2 -MT lib/stream.lo -MD -MP -MF $depbase.Tpo -c -o lib/stream.lo lib/stream.c &&\
mv -f $depbase.Tpo $depbase.Plo

-e 's,[@]LOGDIR[@],"/var/log/openvswitch",g' \
-e 's,[@]RUNDIR[@],"/var/run/openvswitch",g' \
-e 's,[@]DBDIR[@],"/etc/openvswitch",g' \
-e 's,[@]bindir[@],"/usr/bin",g' \

-e 's,[@]pkgdatadir[@],"/usr/share/openvswitch",g') \
> lib/dirs.c.tmp && \
mv lib/dirs.c.tmp lib/dirs.c

/bin/sh ./libtool --tag=CC --mode=compile gcc -std=gnu99 -DHAVE_CONFIG_H -I. -I ./include -I ./include -I ./lib -I ./lib -Wstrict-prototypes -Wall -Wextra -Wno-sign-compare -Wpointer-arith -Wswitch-enum -Wunused-parameter -Wbad-function-cast -Wcast-align -Wmissing-prototypes -Wmissing-field-initializers -fno-strict-aliasing -g -O2 -MT lib/aes128.lo -MD -MP -MF $depbase.Tpo -c -o lib/aes128.lo lib/aes128.c &&\
mv -f $depbase.Tpo $depbase.Plo
